# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
if the original function is concave down, the derivative goes from negative to positive and is
always growing, therefore it's gradient, the second derivative is always positive ^uVnMumXC

you write the function in x, find the derivative, invert, simplify and replace back the initial value  ^ipidMGA4
